 SELECT SUM(cnt) AS cnt,      status_code,      status,      status_name_code  FROM (      SELECT cnt,          INNERS.status_code,           tbcis.Xg_Client_Info.susg_status_decode(INNERS.status_code,           INNERS.end_date,          INNERS.setr_type,          INNERS.status_case,          ?) AS status,          tbcis.Xg_Client_Info.get_susg_status_code(INNERS.status_code,          INNERS.end_date,          INNERS.setr_type,          INNERS.status_case) AS status_name_code      FROM (          SELECT COUNT(*) AS cnt,             ssgs.status_code,              ssgs.end_date,              ssgs.setr_type,              ssgs.status_case          FROM subs_accounts_v suac,              subs_serv_groups susg,              ssg_statuses ssgs         WHERE              suac.maac_ref_num = ?             AND susg.suac_ref_num = suac.ref_num              AND susg.nety_type_code = 'GSM'              AND SYSDATE BETWEEN ssgs.start_date AND NVL(ssgs.end_date, SYSDATE + 1)              AND ssgs.susg_ref_num = susg.ref_num          GROUP BY             ssgs.status_code,              ssgs.end_date,              ssgs.setr_type,              ssgs.status_case)     INNERS)  INNERS2  GROUP BY      INNERS2.status_code,      INNERS2.status,      INNERS2.status_name_code

(SELECT CCRE.REF_NUM             REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_START        PERIOD_START, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_END          PERIOD_END, 
         CCRD.INVO_REF_NUM        INVO_REF_NUM, 
         CCRE.DATE_CREATED        DATE_ORDERED, 
         CCRE.REQUEST_STATUS      STATUS, 
         CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE DATE_COMPLETED, 
         CCRE.USRE_REF_NUM        USRE_REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.OUTPUT_FORMAT       OUTPUT_FORMAT 
  FROM   CCM_REQUESTS CCRE, 
         CCM_REQUEST_DETAILS CCRD 
  WHERE  CCRE.REF_NUM = CCRD.CCRE_REF_NUM 
         AND ((CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE BETWEEN TRUNC((ADD_MONTHS(TRUNC(SYSDATE),-3)),'MONTH') AND SYSDATE) 
               OR CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE IS NULL)) 
 ORDER BY USRE_REF_NUM DESC

         AND CRDE.SUSG_REF_NUM = ?

 ORDER BY USRE_REF_NUM DESC

 ORDER BY USRE_REF_NUM DESC 

(SELECT CCRE.REF_NUM             REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_START        PERIOD_START, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_END          PERIOD_END, 
         CCRD.INVO_REF_NUM        INVO_REF_NUM, 
         CCRE.DATE_CREATED        DATE_ORDERED, 
         CCRE.REQUEST_STATUS      STATUS, 
         CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE DATE_COMPLETED, 
         CCRE.USRE_REF_NUM        USRE_REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.OUTPUT_FORMAT       OUTPUT_FORMAT 
  FROM   CCM_REQUESTS CCRE, 
         CCM_REQUEST_DETAILS CCRD 
  WHERE  CCRE.REF_NUM = CCRD.CCRE_REF_NUM 
         AND CCRE.SESSION_ID IS NOT NULL 
         AND CCRE.SESSION_ID = ? 
         AND ((CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE BETWEEN TRUNC((ADD_MONTHS(TRUNC(SYSDATE),-3)),'MONTH') AND SYSDATE) 
               OR CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE IS NULL)) 
 ORDER BY USRE_REF_NUM DESC 

(SELECT CCRE.REF_NUM             REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_START        PERIOD_START, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_END          PERIOD_END, 
         CCRD.INVO_REF_NUM        INVO_REF_NUM, 
         CCRE.DATE_CREATED        DATE_ORDERED, 
         CCRE.REQUEST_STATUS      STATUS, 
         CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE DATE_COMPLETED, 
         CCRE.USRE_REF_NUM        USRE_REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.OUTPUT_FORMAT       OUTPUT_FORMAT 
  FROM   CCM_REQUESTS CCRE, 
         CCM_REQUEST_DETAILS CCRD 
  WHERE  CCRE.REF_NUM = CCRD.CCRE_REF_NUM 
         AND CCRE.SESSION_ID IS NOT NULL 
         AND CCRE.SESSION_ID = ? 
         AND ((CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE BETWEEN TRUNC((ADD_MONTHS(TRUNC(SYSDATE),-3)),'MONTH') AND SYSDATE) 
               OR CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE IS NULL)) 
 UNION  
 (SELECT CCRE.REF_NUM             REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_START        PERIOD_START, 
         CCRD.PERIOD_END          PERIOD_END, 
         CCRD.INVO_REF_NUM        INVO_REF_NUM, 
         CCRE.DATE_CREATED        DATE_ORDERED, 
         CCRE.REQUEST_STATUS      STATUS, 
         CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE DATE_COMPLETED, 
         CCRE.USRE_REF_NUM        USRE_REF_NUM, 
         CCRD.OUTPUT_FORMAT       OUTPUT_FORMAT 
  FROM   CCM_REQUESTS CCRE, 
         CCM_REQUEST_DETAILS CCRD, 
         CCM_REQUEST_DETAIL_ENTRIES CRDE 
  WHERE  CCRE.REF_NUM = CCRD.CCRE_REF_NUM 
         AND CCRE.CHANNEL_TYPE = 'ITB' 
         AND CCRD.DOCUMENT_TYPE IN ('KER', 'GKER') 
         AND CCRE.REQUEST_TYPE = 'SERV' 
         AND CCRD.REF_NUM = CRDE.CCRD_REF_NUM 
         AND CCRE.SESSION_ID IS NOT NULL 
         AND CCRE.SESSION_ID <> CRDE.SUSG_REF_NUM 
         AND CRDE.SUSG_REF_NUM = ? 
         AND ((CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE BETWEEN TRUNC((ADD_MONTHS(TRUNC(SYSDATE),-3)),'MONTH') AND SYSDATE) 
               OR CCRE.PROCESSING_END_DATE IS NULL) 
         AND (SELECT COUNT(* ) 
              FROM   CCM_REQUEST_DETAIL_ENTRIES CRDE1 
              WHERE  CRDE1.CCRD_REF_NUM = CCRD.REF_NUM) = 1) 
 ORDER BY USRE_REF_NUM DESC

);

Declare pcnter NUMBER:=1000; n NUMBER; PROCEDURE del(pcnt NUMBER) IS begin DELETE FROM dwh_maac_creditratings WHERE date_created < to_date(?,'dd.mm.yyyy') and ROWNUM < pcnt; commit; end; begin SELECT COUNT(*) INTO n FROM dwh_maac_creditratings; LOOP del(pcnter); n:=n-pcnter; EXIT WHEN n<=0; end loop; end; 
Declare pcnter NUMBER:=1000; n NUMBER; PROCEDURE del(pcnt NUMBER) IS begin DELETE FROM dwh_maac_creditratings_WORK WHERE date_created < to_date(?,'dd.mm.yyyy') and ROWNUM < pcnt; commit; end; begin SELECT COUNT(*) INTO n FROM dwh_maac_creditratings_WORK; LOOP del(pcnter); n:=n-pcnter; EXIT WHEN n<=0; end loop; end; 
Declare tot_amt NUMBER := 0.00; function check_deptor_party(p_part_ref_num number) return varchar2 IS result varchar2(1) := 'N'; CURSOR c IS SELECT macv.ref_num, acst.acst_code FROM master_accounts_v macv, account_statuses acst WHERE macv.part_ref_num = p_part_ref_num AND macv.ref_num = acst.acco_ref_num AND (acst.end_date IS NULL OR acst.end_date > SYSDATE); begin for r in c loop IF r.acst_code NOT IN ('CLA','AC','INI','CLP') THEN tot_amt := tot_amt + account_balances.calc_total_outstanding(r.ref_num); ELSE tot_amt := tot_amt + account_balances.calc_amount_ov_unproc(r.ref_num); END IF; end loop; IF tot_amt > 50 THEN result := 'Y'; end if; return result; end; begin ?:=check_deptor_party(?); end;

SELECT     NVL(dico.short_description,dico.description) AS description     ,sudi.start_date + (SELECT NVL(MAX(from_day), 0) FROM call_discount_codes cadc WHERE cadc.ref_num = dico.ref_num) AS start_date     ,dico.discount_code     ,sudi.closed     ,sudi.reason_code     ,CASE WHEN sudi.end_date IS NULL THEN        (SELECT             CASE WHEN MAX(cadc.count_for_months) IS NOT NULL OR MAX(cadc.count_for_days) IS NOT NULL THEN                 CAST (LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(sudi.start_date, NVL(MAX(cadc.count_for_months), 0)) + NVL(MAX(cadc.count_for_days),0)) AS DATE)             ELSE                 MAX(cadc.end_date)             END AS end_date2          FROM              call_discount_codes cadc          WHERE              cadc.dico_ref_num = dico.ref_num)      ELSE          sudi.end_date      END AS end_date     ,dico.ref_num AS dico_ref_num FROM     discount_codes dico     ,subs_discounts sudi WHERE     dico.ref_num = sudi.dico_ref_num     AND sudi.cadc_ref_num IS NULL     AND sudi.susg_ref_num = ? ORDER BY     start_date DESC 
SELECT     NVL(dico.short_description,dico.description) AS description     ,sudi.start_date + (SELECT NVL(MAX(from_day), 0) FROM call_discount_codes cadc WHERE cadc.ref_num = dico.ref_num) AS start_date     ,dico.discount_code AS discount_code     ,CASE WHEN sudi.end_date IS NULL THEN        (SELECT             CASE WHEN MAX(cadc.count_for_months) IS NOT NULL OR MAX(cadc.count_for_days) IS NOT NULL THEN                 CAST (ADD_MONTHS(sudi.start_date, NVL(MAX(cadc.count_for_months), 0)) + NVL(MAX(cadc.count_for_days),0) AS DATE)             ELSE                 MAX(cadc.end_date)             END AS end_date2          FROM              call_discount_codes cadc          WHERE              cadc.dico_ref_num = dico.ref_num)      ELSE          sudi.end_date      END      AS end_date     ,dico.start_date AS sell_start     ,dico.end_date AS sell_end     ,(SELECT description FROM bcc_domain_values WHERE doma_type_code = 'SUDR' AND value_code = sudi.reason_code) AS reason_ended FROM     discount_codes dico     ,subs_discounts sudi WHERE     dico.ref_num = sudi.dico_ref_num     AND sudi.cadc_ref_num IS NULL     AND dico.ref_num = ? 
SELECT     call_type     ,description     ,end_date     ,count_for_months     ,count_for_days FROM     call_discount_codes cadc WHERE     cadc.dico_ref_num = ?

SELECT CCRE.REF_NUM        REF_NUM, 
        CCRD.REF_NUM        CCRD_REF_NUM, 
        CCRE.REQUEST_STATUS STATUS, 
        CCRE.SESSION_ID     SESSION_ID, 
        CCRF.OUTPUT_FORMAT  OUTPUT_FORMAT, 
        CCRD.FILE_DIRECTORY FILE_DIRECTORY, 
        CCRF.FILE_NAME      FILE_NAME, 
        CRDE.SUSG_REF_NUM   SUSG_REF_NUM, 
        CCRE.CREATED_BY     CREATED_BY, 
        CCRD.MAAC_REF_NUM   MAAC_REF_NUM 
 FROM   CCM_REQUESTS CCRE, 
        CCM_REQUEST_DETAILS CCRD, 
        CCM_CCRD_RELATED_FILES CCRF, 
        CCM_REQUEST_DETAIL_ENTRIES CRDE 
 WHERE  CCRE.REF_NUM = ? 
        AND CCRE.CHANNEL_TYPE IN ('ITB','DLG') 
        AND CCRD.REQUEST_TYPE IN ('PRNKER','PRNGKER') 
        AND CCRD.CCRE_REF_NUM = CCRE.REF_NUM 
        AND CCRF.CCRD_REF_NUM = CCRD.REF_NUM 
        AND CRDE.CCRD_REF_NUM(+) = CCRD.REF_NUM

AND MANU.NAME = ? AND FEVA.REF_NUM = TEFE.FEVA_REF_NUM AND TEFE.FEAT_REF_NUM = FEAT.REF_NUM AND FEAT.FEATURE_NAME = 'PROVISIONING METHOD' AND ((PROV.PROV_NAME LIKE 'CSD%' AND TERM.CSD = 1 AND TERM.WAP = 1) OR (PROV.PROV_NAME LIKE 'GPRS%' AND TERM.GPRS = 1 AND TERM.WAP = 1) OR (PROV.PROV_NAME LIKE 'MMS%' AND TERM.GPRS = 1 AND TERM.MMS = 1) OR (PROV.PROV_NAME LIKE 'STREAMING%' AND TERM.GPRS = 1 AND 1 IN (SELECT COUNT (1) FROM TERMINALS TERM_X, TERMINAL_FEATURES TEFE_X, FEATURES FEAT_X WHERE TERM_X.REF_NUM = TERM.REF_NUM AND TERM_X.REF_NUM = TEFE_X.TERM_REF_NUM AND FEAT_X.REF_NUM = TEFE_X.FEAT_REF_NUM AND FEAT_X.FEATURE_NAME = 'STREAMING PROVISIONING')) OR (PROV.PROV_NAME LIKE 'INTERNET%' AND TERM.GPRS = 1 AND 1 IN (SELECT COUNT (1) FROM TERMINALS TERM_X, TERMINAL_FEATURES TEFE_X, FEATURES FEAT_X WHERE TERM_X.REF_NUM = TERM.REF_NUM AND TERM_X.REF_NUM = TEFE_X.TERM_REF_NUM AND FEAT_X.REF_NUM = TEFE_X.FEAT_REF_NUM AND FEAT_X.FEATURE_NAME = 'INTERNET PROVISIONING'))) AND PROV.INDIVIDUAL = 0 AND TERM.MANU_REF_NUM = MANU.REF_NUM AND (TERM.WAP_VERSION = PROV.WAP_VERSION OR (TERM.WAP_VERSION NOT IN (SELECT DISTINCT WAP_VERSION FROM PROVISIONS))) AND INSTR (PROV.CHANNELS, 'TVA') > 0 AND PRAU.TERM_REF_NUM(+) = TERM.REF_NUM
